#
#    Name:     cp936 to Unicode table
#    Unicode version: 2.0
#    Table version: 2.01
#    Table format:  Format A
#    Date:          1/7/2000
#
#    Contact:       Shawn.Steele@microsoft.com
#
#    General notes: none
#
#    Format: Three tab-separated columns
#        Column #1 is the cp936 code (in hex)
#        Column #2 is the Unicode (in hex as 0xXXXX)
#        Column #3 is the Unicode name (follows a comment sign, '#')
#
#    The entries are in cp936 order
#
#    Entries marked EDITED have been added to match:
#    https://www.unicode.org/Public/MAPPINGS/VENDORS/MICSFT/WindowsBestFit/bestfit936.txt
#
